# Meta data

<pre>
Ramon benchmark for Z3
-
Job description: aproximate sort by degree
Job tag: skinny_deg_11
Runner: rise-runner-2
Z3 repo: Z3Prover/z3
Z3 commit: c59c913f00357e9db3f245a2182e245537e5fb20
Z3 branch: skinny
Z3 options: "-T:60 smt.random_seed=11"
Z3 inputs: inputs/QF_NIA_small
Z3 commit message: nlsat: sort clauses by ascending polynomial degree in check(rvalues)

Pre-sort the clauses by polynomial degree (constant for the duration of
check, since the assignment is not modified) and walk them in ascending
order. The first falsified clause encountered then has the smallest
degree, which yields a cheaper conflict lemma. Among falsified clauses
sharing the smallest degree, pick one uniformly at random. Also restore
m_assignment on every return path.

Co-authored-by: Copilot <223556219+Copilot@users.noreply.github.com>

</pre>
